# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="88d92-102">.NET Framework 中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88d92-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="88d92-103">本文列出在 .NET Framework 4.5 和更新版本中已過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88d92-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="88d92-104">型別成員是依元件分組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88d92-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="88d92-105">本文不會列出過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88d92-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="88d92-106">如需過時的類型清單，請參閱[過時的類型](obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="88d92-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
